The phase's own review was real but not exhaustive — **five more data-loss-class bugs lived in windows the fixtures didn't cover**, all fixed on-branch by three build agents (each fix mutation-verified): *(1)* the crash-resume hole — a migration killed after `_ns_move_tree` but before the lock rewrite re-ran as a normal update with Phase-24b preservation silently disabled (tree NEW, lock OLD — the inverse of the adopt-bridge spelling the fixtures used); detection now fires on tree-probe OR an old-spelled lock (`_ns_lock_is_old_spelled`), the derive builds the FULL move map (so the shadow realigns on resume) with a separate `NS_MOVE_PENDING` count, and snapshot candidates union both spellings; *(2)* pack scripts were invisible to the re-trigger probe (core-only enumeration, contradicting its own comment) — a leftover `shared_cli.py` was `git rm`'d by the sweep instead of migrated; probe + T4 scan now share `_ns_vendor_basenames` (core + installed packs); *(3)* `_ns_migrate_settings` built its removal set from ALL template rules (`r.replace()` no-ops on the ~20 non-path rules), permanently stripping still-valid rules from consumer-owned `settings.local.json` (bites loop mode); the set is now vendor-path rules only; *(4)* `--ref` at a pre-namespace tag installed old script bodies (flat/`parent.parent` anchors) into new-layout paths, exit 0 — now era-checked and refused; *(5)* a lockless fresh install over a committed old-layout tree stranded the whole flat vendor tree as an unmanaged duplicate — now refused with `--adopt`→`--update` guidance. Plus: preflight now runs only when real moves are pending (was: hard-blocked every `--update` for a consumer keeping their own file at a shipped basename); `--accept-upstream` accepts the old spelling (key remap); the dry-run stale-ref report excludes everything Sysop owns (was: 112 bogus "fix by hand" entries vs the real run's 2, empirically); the dry-run preservation preview resolves `_work`/`_anc` independently (correct in all three states: normal / adopt-bridge / crash-resume); the pre-commit example's A1/A5 checks re-target the consumer's own `scripts/` (ownership test — the sweep had blanket-renamed them); stale flat-path strings fixed across 12 shipped scripts (the sweep never touched `run_checks/`; T4 structurally can't flag Sysop-owned files); and the CLAUDE.md row re-trimmed to the one-liner convention. **The orchestrator's review of the agent work itself caught two regressions before commit:** the restructure latched `MIGRATION_MODE=1` permanently for the colliding-basename consumer (suppressing the post-overwrite delta report via the `:1319` early-return forever) — now gated on `NS_MOVE_PENDING > 0 || old-spelled lock`, state-derivation done independently twice; and the new fresh-guard refused on a SINGLE colliding basename — now requires ≥2 vendor basenames or 1 + a corroborating Sysop artifact. **Near-leak caught and reversed:** `VIDEO_SCRIPT.md` (announce narration, convention: never tracked) had been committed in the close-out commit; `git rm --cached` before merge, plus a `.git/info/exclude` entry (local-only, no mirror footprint). One PLAUSIBLE finding (migration-mode post-overwrite signal gap in the ancestor-unreachable fallback) filed to the checklist rather than fixed. **Gate: 940 tests green** (928 + 12 new regression tests, all mutation-verified).

## Phase 129 (executed 2026-07-18 — loop-mode public-doc pass: orientation page + highlight across every public surface)

**The gap.** Loop mode (Phase 123) was about to go public carrying only its leg-4 minimum: a README door, the install-modes reference section, one landing-page paragraph, and `install.sh --help`. A coverage survey found it absent from eight surfaces a reader would reasonably reach — the monograph never mentioned the mode exists (§ VI documents plugin-vs-bash but not full-vs-loop), the tutorial had no loop path at all, and the shipped `WORKFLOW.md`/`WORKFLOW_GUIDE.md` never note the mode. The sharpest structural fact: loop mode installs zero local docs (it deliberately skips `install_workflow_docs`), so a loop consumer's *only* orientation is the public docs site — and no orientation page existed. The spec's open question ("where does loop-mode orientation live, given zero shipped root docs") was still unresolved, with the recorded lean "public docs page only."

**What shipped.** The lean, executed. **`docs/loop-mode.md`** is the new orientation home: install (with the loop-correct commit line — no `tasks/`, no `.gitignore` append), what lands vs. what's deliberately lazy (`review_tasks.md` bootstraps on the first audit run, `SYSOP_ISSUES.md` on first capture), the day-one first review, how the loop closes (promotion human-adjudicated, overlay-durable, mechanization, demotion), where enforcement lives (the pre-commit hook's check slots + the CI template running `run_checks` — no merge gate), the additive `--update --mode full` growth path, an honest validation note, and explicit non-goals. Everything else now routes there: the README door + a new Documentation row + the Quickstart link; the landing page § IV grew a second start path (its own `--mode loop` install block + copy button) and the read-next band went 4 → 6 tiles (**On-ramp · Just the loop**, plus **Evidence · One rule, end to end** — previously footer-only); the monograph gained § VI "Two install modes: full and loop" and a § IV pullquote line; getting-started gained the install fork + a maintain-section pointer; `packs.md` states packs are entirely loop-side content; `one-rule.md`, `history.md`, `configuration.md`, `WORKFLOW.md` § 8, and `WORKFLOW_GUIDE.md` each carry one calibrated cross-reference.

**The validation citation (decision recorded).** Leg 5's dogfood is real evidence, and public copy now carries it — deliberately de-identified: "run once, end-to-end, against a real ~60k-line open-source codebase — a freshly mechanized convention caught an instance no review round had filed," stated with its limit ("one run on one project: evidence the mechanism works, not a benchmark"). The target stays unnamed on every public surface, this entry included; the full named writeup is reserved as announce-time material.

**Adversarial review (self-imposed, pre-merge — two independent fresh-context reviewers, not forks; lenses: de-identification + claim honesty, and factual accuracy vs. `install.sh` + links).** Each surfaced one real HIGH. Reviewer 1: the orientation page's validation note named the dogfood target's implementation language — the one stack detail the de-identified formula everywhere else omits — fixed to the formula verbatim; also "code the model had never seen" (unverifiable for an open-source target) → the accurate "code the model didn't write," and history.md's "early cold readers" reworded to disclose they are fresh-context model readers simulating adopters, not humans. Reviewer 2: "`run_checks` bites at the pre-commit hook" was factually wrong — the shipped hook is a self-contained check-slot skeleton that never invokes `run_checks` (which runs in the CI template and the audit skills' pre-scan); fixed in the new page, the new WORKFLOW.md note, *and* the same pre-existing conflation in `install-and-update.md` § Install modes. Also fixed on its findings: Round semantics ("its own round" → same-day audit runs share a Round), overlays described as landing at install (they're created by the first promotion), § III/§ IV machinery attribution in the monograph, the five-skill enumeration in § VI, a plugin-guidance gap (loop installs need no plugin), and four smaller wording nits. Both reviewers verified the full install inventory, every skill-behavior claim, and every added link/anchor clean.

**Gate.** 940 tests green before and after the review fixes (doc-currency guards included). Landed via branch → PR → squash-merge to protected `main`. Dev-repo only for now: the new `docs/loop-mode.md` blob links resolve publicly only once loop mode and this pass ship in the same public snapshot — which is exactly the loop-only item's remaining leg (b), the next deliberate mirror push.

## Phase 130 (executed 2026-07-18 — pre-push loop-mode polish: the cheap leg-5 defects + the dogfood-naming mirror gate)

**The call.** The next mirror push is loop mode's public debut (public sits at Phase 122; the delta is 123–129). The leg-5 dogfood had filed 8 defects routed to "the next install.sh/run_checks-touching phase" — but three of them blemish exactly the surface the push headlines, and each is under an hour. Shipping the debut with known day-one warts we could fix first fails the measure-twice test, so the cheap three landed as a pre-push bundle; the five real design/doc items (1, 3, 4, 5, 8) stay parked per the checklist's own routing.

**What shipped.** (a) **Leg-5 defect 7a — the sneaky one, and not loop-specific:** `core/companion/convention_map.md`'s section header still read `scripts/*.sh, scripts/hooks/*`, but Phase 128 moved consumer scripts to `sysop/scripts/**` — and `/codebase-review` glob-matches section headers to scope rules, so the entire shell-script/git-hooks convention section had silently stopped applying to every post-128 consumer (a Phase-128 regression in the shipped map). Header now covers both `sysop/scripts/*.sh` + `sysop/scripts/hooks/*` (the installed payload) and the original `scripts/*` globs (consumer-authored scripts + pre-migration installs). (b) **Leg-5 defect 2:** loop mode skipped `ensure_runtime_gitignore` entirely on the claim that no runtime dir can exist in loop mode — false for `.pending-docs/`, which `/codebase-review` + `/security-audit` Step 8 promotion-deferral writes. The function now narrows its `want` set to `.pending-docs/` alone in loop mode (the full four-entry declaration stays first so the runtime-gitignore drift-guard regex still parses it), the pipeline calls it unconditionally, and the leg-3 footprint test flipped from "no `.gitignore`" to "`.pending-docs/` exactly once, zero dead lifecycle entries." (c) **Leg-5 defect 7b:** `/test-audit`'s Step 5 actuator routed accepted recommendations to `/intake`, which loop mode doesn't install; the skill now keys on `.claude/sysop.lock` `mode: loop` and offers copy-pasteable entries for the project's own tracker instead. (d) **Mirror-gate insurance:** `make_public_mirror.sh`'s verify block gains Pass 1c — a must-be-empty grep for the leg-5 dogfood target's name, enforcing the 2026-07-18 naming rule (target de-identified on every public surface until the staged maintainer report is delivered; the pass documents its own expiry). The rule held structurally already (the name lives only in mirror-excluded files — this entry deliberately doesn't carry it either, since this file ships); now the gate says so on every future cut.

**Gate.** 940 tests green (the flipped loop-footprint test included). Landed via branch → PR → squash-merge to protected `main`, immediately ahead of the mirror push it exists to clean up for.

**Update (same day, 2026-07-18 — both mirror pushes executed; loop mode's public debut).** Full gate on the exact pushed tree (snapshot of `5ef046b`): **Pass 1a / 1b / 1c / 3 empty**; Pass 2 = 1 new hit (the Phase-122 mirror-record paragraph in this file — ratified changelog class); Pass 2b = the TECH-0007 consumer-provenance class accepted at the 07-17 tester push; suite green **inside the mirror tree** (915 passed, 4 history-dependent skips — tests that need multi-commit history can't run in a single-commit snapshot). Tester: force-pushed `wade-cms/sysop-tester` main `4f28698` → `0d5a88f` (Phase 127 → 130) + the refresh note to Snapshot-updates Discussion #1. Public: append-via-PR (`getsysop/sysop#13`, pytest green there) squash-merged **`574b6a3`** — public moves Phase 122 → 130, so loop mode, its orientation page, and the `sysop/` vendor-namespace migration all shipped publicly at once. Pages `built` on the first attempt; live-content probes: the landing page serves the `--mode loop` start path + "Just the loop" tile, and the `docs/loop-mode.md` links now resolve (the Phase-129 gate condition, closed). The loop-only checklist item is resolved to the archive; the staged maintainer report to the dogfood target — the naming-rule unlock — is refiled as its own open item.

**Update 2 (same day, 2026-07-18 — round-4 cold read against the freshly-public surfaces).** Two zero-context readers, identical round-3 brief re-run verbatim per that file's comparison instruction (`tools/COLD_READ_ROUND4_FABLE.md`). **The round-3 tipping condition fired:** both still maybe-later on the full lifecycle, but both commit to a `--mode loop` install on a side project "this month" (round 3's readers would install nothing), and the #1 full-lifecycle blocker moved off the product to social proof — announce-gated, not code-fixable. Round-3 items confirmed landed: loop mode (found unprompted, chosen), the `sysop/` footprint (the "visceral no" not raised), `one-rule.md`, `history.md`. Both readers went deeper than any prior round (cloned the public repo, ran the suite cold — green, real installs into scratch repos) and surfaced the first-touch defects Phase 131 fixes.

## Phase 131 (executed 2026-07-18 — round-4 first-touch bundle: the quickstart `fatal:`, the permission disclosure, and three small doc drifts)

**The trigger.** The round-4 cold read's one confirmed defect and four small frictions, all on the first ten minutes of a new adopter's experience — the surface both readers said "undoes the credibility the 919-test suite earned." Items (a)–(e) of the round-4 checklist bundle; (f) demo-above-the-fold and (g) the funnel-inversion decision stay open (announce planning / Wade's call).

**What shipped.** (a) **The quickstart `fatal:` (both readers reproduced it, build-session repro confirmed):** `seed_claude_md_stub` — Phase 123's section-level append-if-absent CLAUDE.md seeder — now runs in **both modes**, not just loop. Full-mode installs on a bare repo previously left no `CLAUDE.md`, so the documented first post-install command (`git add .claude/ sysop/ tasks/ CLAUDE.md .gitignore`) died with exit 128 and *nothing staged*. The audit skills consume the same three scope sections in full mode, and the stub composes with the §6.1 bootstrap / `/intake` (their sections append later), so seeding is correct, not just convenient; the stub's loop-specific wording generalized. (b) **Install-time permission disclosure:** `install_permissions` now states the allow-list's blast radius out loud on every path (fresh, merge, dry-run) — full mode names the `git push origin` / `git push --force-with-lease` grants and the delete-any-rule remedy; loop mode states its no-push/merge/rebase subset. `docs/install-and-update.md`'s settings paragraph gains the same disclosure plus the fact reader 2 missed: **the allow-list is already tiered by mode** (14-rule loop subset). (c) **PEP-668 PyYAML guidance:** README + getting-started now lead with the project-venv install (`.venv/bin/pip install pyyaml`) and state that `run_checks.sh` resolves the repo's `.venv` on its own (verified against the script — PATH-prefix + venv-python preference) and that bare `pip install` refuses on externally-managed Pythons. (d) `CONTRIBUTING.md`'s friction-log path corrected to `sysop/SYSOP_ISSUES.md` (Phase-128 drift) with the loop-mode lazy-create noted. (e) `docs/history.md`'s "750+ tests" → dated "900+ by mid-July" (a dated count doesn't rot like a current-state count; the Phase-118 ratchet covers README/landing, not the timeline). Bundle rider: `docs/loop-mode.md`'s commit line gains `.gitignore` — stale the same morning it shipped, since Phase 130 made loop mode append `.pending-docs/` (our own drift, caught in this pass).

**Gate.** +4 tests (`tests/test_install_first_touch.py`, real-installer E2E: the quickstart line succeeds **verbatim** on a bare repo, authored-CLAUDE.md append-not-rewrite, both modes' disclosure lines assert — including that the loop settings really carry no push grant), 944 total green. Landed via branch → PR → squash-merge to protected `main`; mirrors re-pushed the same day so the fixes reach adopters before announce.
